       78 +export async function POST(req: Request) {                    
       79 +  try {                                                       
       80 +    const auth = await requireAuth();                         
       81 +    await connectMongo();                                     
       82 +                                                              
       83 +    let raw: unknown;                                         
       84 +    try {                                                     
       85 +      raw = await req.json();                                 
       86 +    } catch {                                                 
       87 +      return jsonError(400, "VALIDATION_ERROR", "Body must be 
          +JSON");                                                       
       88 +    }                                                         
       89 +                                                              
       90 +    const parsed = createBodySchema.safeParse(raw);           
       91 +    if (!parsed.success) {                                    
       92 +      const first = parsed.error.issues[0];                   
       93 +      return jsonError(400, "VALIDATION_ERROR", first.message,
          + {                                                            
       94 +        field: first.path.join("."),                          
       95 +      });                                                     
       96 +    }                                                         
       97 +    const body = parsed.data;                                 
       98 +                                                              
       99 +    const category = await Category.findById(body.categoryId);
      100 +    if (!category || !category.active) {                      
      101 +      return jsonError(400, "VALIDATION_ERROR", "Unknown or in
          +active categoryId", {                                         
      102 +        field: "categoryId",                                  
      103 +      });                                                     
      104 +    }                                                         
      105 +                                                              
      106 +    let doc;                                                  
      107 +    try {                                                     
      108 +      doc = await CatalogItem.create({                        
      109 +        name: body.name,                                      
      110 +        categoryId: category._id,                             
      111 +        categoryName: category.name,                          
      112 +        programName: category.programName,                    
      113 +        defaultUnit: body.defaultUnit,                        
      114 +        estimatedValuePerUnit: body.estimatedValuePerUnit,    
      115 +        aliases: body.aliases ?? [],                          
      116 +        active: true,                                         
      117 +      });                                                     
      118 +    } catch (e: unknown) {                                    
      119 +      // Duplicate (categoryId, name, active) per the model's 
          +case-insensitive                                              
      120 +      // compound unique index.                               
      121 +      if ((e as { code?: number })?.code === 11000) {         
      122 +        return jsonError(                                     
      123 +          409,                                                
      124 +          "CONFLICT",                                         
      125 +          "An item with this name already exists in that categ
          +ory",                                                         
      126 +          { field: "name" },                                  
      127 +        );                                                    
      128 +      }                                                       
      129 +      throw e;                                                
      130 +    }                                                         
      131 +                                                              
      132 +    const summary = `${auth.displayName} added ${doc.name} (${
          +doc.categoryName}) to the catalog`;                           
      133 +    await recordEvent(                                        
      134 +      "item.created",                                         
      135 +      { actorId: auth.userId, fullName: auth.fullName, display
          +Name: auth.displayName },                                     
      136 +      { id: String(doc._id), label: doc.name },               
      137 +      summary,                                                
      138 +    );                                                        
      139 +                                                              
      140 +    return NextResponse.json(                                 
      141 +      { item: doc.toJSON() as unknown as WireCatalogItem },   
      142 +      { status: 201 },                                        
      143 +    );                                                        
      144 +  } catch (err) {                                             
      145 +    return jsonErrorFromException(err);                       
      146 +  }

  One manual step you have to do for the "force full name" part:

  Go to the Clerk Dashboard → User & Authentication → Email, Phone, Username (in
   some Clerk versions it's under "Personal information"). Toggle:
  - First name → Required
  - Last name → Required

  Save. The <SignUp /> component reads required fields from the dashboard, so
  flipping that toggle is what actually enforces it. There's no code-only way to
   require fields that the dashboard says are optional. Once flipped, new
  signups can't proceed without filling both names.

  Test in browser:
  1. /log/quick → "+ New item" → fill the form → confirm it appears in the grid
  + auto-selected
  2. /history → confirm the new "added X to the catalog" event shows up
  3. /profile → confirm Notifications row is gone
  4. /sign-up → confirm it renders (sign out first if needed)

  When you're happy, say the word and I'll commit + push so Vercel rebuilds.

● Pushed 60498ae. Vercel rebuilds in ~2 min.

  On the Gemini API key — what to change:

  The variable name is GOOGLE_API_KEY (not GEMINI_API_KEY — common confusion).
  Two places to update:

  1. Locally, edit .env:
  GOOGLE_API_KEY=your-new-key-here
  1. Then restart the dev server (Ctrl+C then npm run dev) — Next reads env vars
   at boot, hot-reload doesn't pick up env changes.
  2. On Vercel (for the live deploy):
    - Vercel Dashboard → your hack-davis2026 project → Settings → Environment 
  Variables
    - Find GOOGLE_API_KEY → click ⋯ → Edit → paste new key → Save
    - Vercel won't redeploy automatically on env changes. Either: hit
  Deployments → latest → ⋯ → Redeploy, or push any commit (the next push will
  use the new key).

  Heads up on the new key: if it's still on the free tier, you'll hit the same
  per-minute / per-day caps. Enabling billing on the Google Cloud project tied
  to the new key is what actually unblocks heavy testing.

  Local refresh checklist for the other two changes (after Turbopack picks them
  up):
  - /history → type something in the search box → feed filters
  - /sign-in and /sign-up → form button is now green, focus rings green, Inter
  font

● Pushed f5b808a..eae247e — Vercel is deploying now. Test on
  https://hack-davis2026.vercel.app once the green ✓ shows.

  What changed:

  1. AI lbs items — catalog's defaultUnit is now the source of truth (no more AI
   overriding lbs → count). For any lbs item, the AI no longer guesses qty or
  value; the row lands in Review with both fields blank, and save is blocked
  until the volunteer fills them in.
  2. Partial-match review — Photo now only errors when the AI saw nothing. If
  even one item is detected (matched or not), you land in Review where you can:
    - Edit / delete the detected items as before
    - + Add item (top of page) — opens the New Item modal; new lbs items also
  start blank
    - + New category (top of page, plus the existing footer link inside each
  row's category dropdown)
  3. Strict validation everywhere — Quick Pick, Manual Entry, and AI Review all
  now reject empty / 0 quantity and empty / 0 dollar value with a toast.
  4. Auth pages re-themed — Clerk now picks up explicit formButtonPrimary,
  formFieldInput focus, social-button, divider, and link overrides so the form
  pane actually looks green-on-white instead of stock blue Clerk.

● Type check is clean. Closing the remaining tasks.

● Three changes landed; type check clean.

  - History (src/app/(app)/history/page.tsx) — stripped the Sheet, edit/delete
  handlers, and click-to-open. Read-only feed with search, bucketing, and the
  same toast surface.
  - AI not-in-catalog (src/lib/ai/gemini.ts) — root cause: the unmatched branch
  dropped the AI's category guess on the floor even though Gemini is
  enum-constrained to your active categories. Now I look up the AI's category in
   args.categories and populate categoryId + programName (+ defaultUnit if AI
  didn't supply one). So "blue jeans" lands in Review with a real green-pill
  category like Apparel, the volunteer can keep it, change it via the chip, or
  hit "+ New category" — and the save validation passes.
  - Review row UX (src/app/(app)/log/review/page.tsx) — softened the "Not in
  catalog" pill from red→amber (it's a warning, not a save blocker anymore) and
  added a one-line Subtle hint under the chips telling the volunteer to tap the
  category and set the value before saving.

  Quick Pick and Review already support add/remove/edit pre-save and
  createDonations writes donation.created audit events that the History page
  renders — no change there. Ready for vercel timeee whenever you are.

✻ Churned for 6m 29s

● Three changes landed; type check clean.

  - History (src/app/(app)/history/page.tsx) — stripped the Sheet, edit/delete
  handlers, and click-to-open. Read-only feed with search, bucketing, and the
  same toast surface.
  - AI not-in-catalog (src/lib/ai/gemini.ts) — root cause: the unmatched branch
  dropped the AI's category guess on the floor even though Gemini is
  enum-constrained to your active categories. Now I look up the AI's category in
   args.categories and populate categoryId + programName (+ defaultUnit if AI
  didn't supply one). So "blue jeans" lands in Review with a real green-pill
  category like Apparel, the volunteer can keep it, change it via the chip, or
  hit "+ New category" — and the save validation passes.
  - Review row UX (src/app/(app)/log/review/page.tsx) — softened the "Not in
  catalog" pill from red→amber (it's a warning, not a save blocker anymore) and
  added a one-line Subtle hint under the chips telling the volunteer to tap the
  category and set the value before saving.

  Quick Pick and Review already support add/remove/edit pre-save and
  createDonations writes donation.created audit events that the History page
  renders — no change there. Ready for vercel timeee whenever you are.

          +id));

● Pushed fb21423 to origin/main. Vercel will redeploy.

  What landed:

  - AI Review — not-in-catalog rows now get a dashed-outline "Save to catalog"
  button next to the amber pill. Tapping opens the New Item modal preloaded with
   the AI's name/category/unit/per-unit value; on save the row's itemId fills
  in, the warning clears, and saving the batch works. Matched rows get a small
  pencil next to the item name to edit the underlying catalog row. The category
  dropdown grows a pencil per category (edit only — no trash anywhere in this
  flow, per the ask).
  - Quick Pick — pencil + trash on every item tile (wrapper became a clickable
  <div> so the action buttons can sit inside without nesting in a parent
  <button>). Pencil + trash next to each category section header. Both deletes
  are confirmed via window.confirm. Item edits propagate to any selected row's
  denormalized name/unit/price; category edits propagate to all items under that
   category.
  - Manual Entry — when the typed name doesn't resolve to an existing catalog
  row, a "Save this item to the catalog" checkbox appears (defaulted on). On
  submit the catalog item is created first; the new itemId is then attached to
  the donation. If the catalog create 409s, the donation submission is aborted
  cleanly so the volunteer can uncheck and retry.
  - Backend — new PATCH/DELETE /api/catalog/:id mirroring categories/[id].
  Soft-deletes via active:false, emits item.archived on delete, no audit on
  PATCH (matches the category unit-only fall-through since CONTRACTS §3 doesn't
  enumerate item.renamed).

   https://hack-davis2026.vercel.app/sign-in. Existing router.push("/sign-in")

✻ Baked for 6m 14s

❯ I have new gemini api what do I do. Explain again                             

● You need to update the GOOGLE_API_KEY env var in two places:

  1. Local .env file (for npm run dev and seed scripts)

  Open /mnt/c/Users/subha/desktop/projects/hackdavis-26/HackDavis2026/.env, find
   the line:

  GOOGLE_API_KEY=...old-key...

  Replace with the new key. Save. Restart npm run dev if it's running (env is
  read at boot).

  2. Vercel project env vars (for the live hack-davis2026.vercel.app deployment)

  Go to: vercel.com → your project → Settings → Environment Variables

  Find GOOGLE_API_KEY, click Edit, paste the new key, save. Make sure it's set
  for Production (and Preview/Development if you want previews to work too).

  Then redeploy so the new env takes effect — easiest path: in the Vercel
  dashboard, Deployments → latest → ⋯ → Redeploy. Or push any commit and it'll
  auto-deploy.

  Verify it works

  After redeploy, hit the AI photo flow on the live site and try a photo. If the
   key is bad you'll see an error toast on the photo screen ("Could not match
  item to catalog" or a 500). If it matches an item, you're good.

  Want me to walk through anything else — e.g., if you want to paste the key
  into the local .env for me, or if you'd like a vercel env CLI command instead
  of the dashboard?

● Pushed 35a2f51. Vercel will redeploy.

  What landed:

  - History now records catalog edits —
    - PATCH on a catalog item snapshots name / category / unit / price / aliases
   before save and emits an item.updated row whose summary lists exactly what
  changed, e.g. "Subhan N. updated Tea (renamed Tea -> Earl Grey, moved to 
  Pantry, price $4.00 -> $4.50)". No-op edits (body included a field but the
  value didn't change) skip emission.
    - PATCH on a category that only changes defaultUnit now emits
  category.updated ("Subhan N. updated category Beverages (unit count -> lbs)")
  instead of falling through silently. Name changes still go through the
  existing category.renamed path.
    - Both new event types are added to AuditEventType in types.ts AND the
  AUDIT_EVENT_TYPES enum in the Mongo model — without the enum the schema
  validator would reject them.
  - Reports — Q2 removed — Preset union, PRESETS array, and the case "Q2":
  branch in rangeForPreset are all gone. The chip row now reads This month · 
  Last month · YTD · Custom.

❯ Hey, on mobile/ipad when I use the AI image mode. I am only able to use my    
  camera while on desktop I am able to only provide images from my gallery. Can 
   you fix this                                                                 

  Searched for 1 pattern, read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

● Found it. The <input> has capture="environment" which forces mobile browsers
  to skip the gallery and open the camera directly, while desktop just ignores
  it and shows the file picker. Removing the attribute lets mobile show the
  native chooser (Take Photo / Photo Library) and desktop continue with the file
   picker.

● Pushed c0598bc. Vercel will redeploy.

  Root cause: the hidden <input type="file"> had capture="environment". Mobile
  browsers obey it (camera only, gallery hidden); desktop ignores it (no native
  camera, just file picker). So each platform got the wrong half of the
  experience.

  Fix: drop the attribute. Now —

  - iOS / iPadOS / Android — tapping the dropzone or the bottom CTA opens the
  native chooser ("Take Photo or Video" / "Photo Library" / "Choose Files"), so
  you can either capture a new photo or pick one from your gallery.
  - Desktop — keeps the existing file picker (no behavior change there).
  - Copy — the dropzone now reads "Tap to add a photo / Take a new photo or 
  choose from your gallery" and the sticky CTA reads "Add Photo" instead of
  "Open Camera".

  Test it by going to /log/photo on your phone after Vercel redeploys — tapping
  should bring up the native sheet with both options.
